                                                  <div data-reactid="5">
                                                    <li data-reactid="6">
                                                      <p data-reactid="7">
                                                        Melody was great.  She was there to meet us.  The house was great for what we needed.  The space for a family of 6 was great for us.  The master bathroom 2nd shower head was not working and we had an issue with the power going out in a portion of the house.  We contacted Melody immediately and she was willing to send an electrician out immediately.  We found that having the lights on and using the microwave seemed to turn off the power.  If you stay on a Tuesday be aware that the landscapers are there.  Caught us off guard to open the garage and they were there and asked to use the garage to get to the backyard.  Let me feeling uneasy with out stuff in the house. I called Melody immediately and she confirmed that yes they were there on Tuesdays.  Only thing I would recommend is adding thick memory foams on the bed.  The master bed was too firm for us but we dealt with it.  The second main room with the full/queen bed was okay.  However the pseudo 3rd room with a mattress on the floor was the worst and hardest one - it was commented that sleeping on the carpet may have been a better nights sleep.  The long ottoman twin bed next to the floor mattress had a topper so it was not as hard.  It worked for my 9 year old but was odd that it was not a true twin mattress bed.  Again all in all I would stay again if the bed accommodations was addressed.  The location was perfect and the neighborhood was great.  Loved it and would return!  Thanks Melody!

                                                    My place is close to the beach, family-friendly activities, nightlife, and public transport. You’ll love my place because of the high ceilings, the views, the location, and the ambiance.                                                   <div data-reactid="3">
                                                    This is the first time this house has been available for renting.  It is a beautiful mid-century modern bungalow (about 900 sq. ft.) walking distance to Doheney Beach and Dana Point Harbor.  Completely renovated with new foam roof with great insulation, motorized awning, laminate wood floors throughout, Quartz countertops, marble dining table, Elfa closets, and travertine bathroom. It is super clean and the third room looks out onto a lush garden.  The property is fronted with floor to ceiling windows, a wonderful balcony for morning coffee, and a huge garage.  The bungalow is located in the rejuvenated Lantern Village - at the quiet end, surrounded by single family homes rather than multifamily rental units.  Also, the home sits below the St. Edward the Confessor Catholic Church.  It's a great quiet neighborhood to take long walks to and on the beach or relax on the deck and listen to the birds chirping.  Partying at this property will not be permitted. 

Notes from guests:
"Everything was amazing. Thank you sooooo much! My family will definitely be staying here when they come visit again. The fireworks view from the deck was perfect."

"We love the house!  The pictures don't do it justice."

This lovely San Clemente house close to San clemente beaches and shopping centers where you can experience the great public beaches, restaurants, shops and parks with tennis court and golf course. Due to our convenient location which is half way between Los Angeles and San Diego, North Orange County / LA attractions (Disneyland, Universal Studios Hollywood, Knott's Berry Farm) and San Diego attractions (Sea World, San Diego Zoo, La Jolla) are both only an hour drive away.

Our guests also like watching HBO and other HD channels as well as streaming Netflix movies using our Wifi-connected blu-ray player. 

This house has total of 6 beds: King bed(sleeps 2), Queen bed (sleeps 2), Two twin beds (sleep 2), Two sofa sleepers each sleeps 1-2 adult or 2 kids. So this house can comfortably accommodate up to 10 guests.

For your convenience, house comes with washer/dryer, laundry detergents, towels, and hand/dish soaps as well.
